 The most pure gold 24 carat (99
 9 pratishat shuddh) hota he
 But it never creates jewelery
 kyonki yah bahut mulaayam hota he
 Metal is mixed in gold to bring the gold into different shapes
 isiilie bazaaron main 23, 22 or 18 jaise carat kii julri milti hai
 You can identify the gold carat from the hallmark written on the jewelery: You can find information on the Bureau of Indian Standards website http: / / www
 bis
 org
 in / cert / hallbiscert
 You can also try visiting htm
 carat ÷ 24 × 100maan len aapaki julri 22 carat kii he to (22 ÷ 24 × 100) hue 91
 6, so your gold purity is 91
 6 pratishat baaki 8
 34 percent contains metal in it
 jo ki julri ko shape main laane ke liye jaruri he
 The price of 10 grams of 24 carat gold is 32,885 and if you are buying 22 carats of jewelery then look at this formula to get its price
 (julri kii keemat × gram main uskaa vazan + mekking charjez + 3 pratishat GST) aap is formul se julri kii sahi keemat nikaal sakate hai
 Price of 10 grams of gold - 32,885 (dividing it by 10 will cost 1 gram of Rs
 3,288) 22 carat yani (9
 16 gold) will cost = 3,288 × 9
 16 = 30,118 rupee Now add the making charges of goldsmith, 3 percent GST - let's say making charges is 10 percent, so the tenth of 30,118 became 3,011 (30,118 + 3,011 = 33,129)
 Now 3 percent of this total amount is 993 rupees
 to total hua 34,122 rupee
 That is why always keep in mind what price you are buying gold in carat
 kyonki kai baar 18 carat kii julri 23 carat ke daamon main bech kar aapke saath dhokhaa kiya jaataa he

 به قلم شبنمم xxrep 5 👇 وقتی پای پرسپولیس در میان باشد ، خانوم بودن میشه یه حسرت
 
 
 باید گذشت و خطر کرد و مرزهای عاشقی رو جا به جا کرد، نمیشه یه روز تاریخیِ دیگه هم کنج خونه بشینیم و حسرتامون رو بغل کنیم
 
 بازم استرس و ریسک، بازم ریش و گریم و لباس پسرونه بازم تغییر هویتی که با تمام این محدودیت ها عاشقش هستیم لیلی و زینب دیروز یه بار دیگه واسه آرزوشون راهی استادیومی شدن که هیچ شباهتی به اسمش نداره
 
 
 یکی رد شد ، یکی بازداشت
 
 
 اینکه نتونی توی رویایی ترین شب پرسپولیسیا خوشحال باشی و توی وزرا جنگ اعصاب داشته باشی تاوان عاشقیه 😒❤ و تو لیلی عزیزم با اینکه یه بار دیگه نماینده ی دخترای ریش دار رو سکوها بودی
 
 
 اما همه میدونن که چقدر استرس برای دستگیری احتمالی از لذت و شادیت کم کرد
 
 
 مدام مجبور به تغییر دادن جایگاه بشی و حتی تا لحظه ی ترک استادیوم در حال تعقیب برای دستگیریت باشن
 
 
 کی حاضره وقتی میدونه شب لذت بخشش ممکنه اینجور عذاب آور بشه و بازم خطر کنه؟ فقط یه عاشق
 
 
 وقتی این درهای لعنتی به روی زنان این سرزمین باز شد ، ما یادمون نمیره که راحتی و لذتمون رو مدیون فداکاری شماییم❤🙏 
 بهتون افتخار میکنم و مطمئنم انتهای این راه پیروزی از آن ماست✌ پ

 ' uttar pradesh main samaajawaadee party (sapa) ne shandaar vaapasi kii he
 It has won 226 seats while Bahujan Samaj Party (BSP) has reduced to 80 seats
 bhaajapa 47 or congress 38 siten paakar tisare or chauthe sthaan par he
 Other candidates have got 12 seats
 sapa kii is aitihaasik jeet kaa shrey pradesh adhyaksh akhilesh yadav ko diya ja rahaa he, jinhone kadi mehnat kii or party kaa rangarup badalane main ahm bhoomika nibhaai lekin yah lagbhag saaf ho gaya he ki mulaayam singh yadav hi mukhyamantri banenge
 As soon as the polling started in the morning, the cycle gained such momentum that it had crossed the magic figure of 202 required for the majority and it was currently close to creating history by winning 226 seats
 iske vipareet hathi kii chaal shuru se hi sust rahi or jaise-jaise nattejey saamne aae vah 80 ke aankade par pahunchakar bedam ho gai
 It was speculated that the SP would emerge as the largest party but it was not even speculated to the SP leaders that it would cross the 220 mark
 varsh 2007 main chunaav main kul 97 siten jeetne vaali sapa ke is pradarshan ne raajnneetik panditon ko chaunkaa kar rakh diya
 On the other hand, the BSP, which had formed a government on its own for the first time by winning a handsome 206 seats in the last election, had a dismal performance
 sapa ko mili baari jeet ke liye janata ko dhanyavad dete hue akhilesh yadav ne kaha ki janata ne jati-dharm se upar uthakar sapa par vishwaas vyakt kiya he
 His party's government will try its best to live up to the expectations of the people
 unhone kaha, "sapa sarkaar banane ke baad apana puraa kaa puraa ghoshnaptr lagu karegi, jisase uttar pradesh khushhaali or vikaas ke raste par ja sake
 " akhilesh ne kaha, "kal (buudhvaar) party sansadeey dal kii baithak hogi
 After the meeting it will be decided when to stake claim to form the government
 " Asked about support, Akhilesh stated clearly, "we will not take support of any mafia
" " unhone kaha, "kanoon evam vyavastha ke mudde par hamen puure chunaav ke dauraan janata ko safai deni padi, lekin ham janata ko bharosa dilaate hai ki sapa kii sarkaar main jo vyakti kanoon todega uske khilaaf kathor karwai kii jaaegi
 " akhilesh ne kaha, "na to kisi hathi kii murti ko chhedaa jayega or na hi mukhyamantri mayawati kii kisi murti ko todaa jayega
 Our government will not take action under the spirit of revenge
 " unhone yah bhi kaha, "agar parkon or smarakon kii khaali padi jagah main shikshan santhaan yaa aspataal khul jaaen to isse logon ko phayda hoga
 " mukhyamantri koun banegaa, ke sawaal par akhilesh ne kaha, "puri party yahi chaahati he ki netaa ji (mulaayam) mukhyamantri bane, isliye vahi banenge
 " chunaav main pradarshan se niraash bhaajapa ke liye haalanki tisare sthaan par aana raahat kii baat ho sakati he, lekin pradesh kii raajnneeti main puri taiyaari ke saath apane 'yuvaraj' rahul gandhi ko utaarne vaali congress ke liye parinaam bahut bada jhatka he
 The Congress has lost all seats in Rae Bareli district
 raibareli party kii rashtriya adhyaksh sonia gandhi kaa sansadeey kshetra he
 Rahul Gandhi has taken responsibility for the disappointing performance of the Congress
 saath hi rahul ne yah bhi kaha ki pradesh main congress kii buniyaad kamjor he jabaki hawa samaajawaadee party (sapa) ke paksh main thi
 Speaking to reporters here, Rahul said, "I fought, so this responsibility is mine
 hamane acchhee ladaai ladi lekin parinaam achche nahin rahe
 "he said," i promised the people of Uttar Pradesh that i would be seen with the poor and on the streets
 meraa kaam jari rahegaa
 My efforts will continue to strengthen the Congress in Uttar Pradesh
 " On the reasons for the disappointing performance of the party, Rahul said that it cannot be said immediately
 "ek yaa do kaaran bahut spasht hai
 The foundation of the Congress in the state is weak
 jab tak ham ise thik nahin karenge, kamajori bani rahegi
 "he said," The mood of the people was in favor of SP, which is not good for us and also not good for the people of Uttar Pradesh
 "tippaniyan Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) president Nitin Gadkari said the results of Uttar Pradesh were contrary to expectations, but also said that SP had the advantage of being the main opposition party there
 gadakari ne yahaan samvaadadaataaon ko sambodhit karte hue kaha, "uttar pradesh main do dalon ke bich voton kaa dhruvikaran ho gaya
 There was an atmosphere against the BSP, which the SP succeeded in taking advantage of
 jab do partiyon ke bich voton kaa dhruvikaran hota he to nattejey aise hi aate hai
 The results were not found here as expected
 " The credit for this historic victory of SP is being given to the state president Akhilesh Yadav, who worked hard and played an important role in changing the look of the party but it is almost clear that Mulayam Singh Yadav will be the chief minister
 subah jaise hi matdaan armbh hua usee samay se cycle ne aisi raftaar pakadi kii usne bahumat ke liye aavashyak 202 ke jaadui aankade ko paar kar hi dam liya or vah philhal 226 siten jitkar itihaas rachane ke kareeb pahunch gai
 In contrast, the elephant's movement remained sluggish from the beginning and as the results came out, it reached breathless figures of 80
 anumaan lagaaya gaya tha ki sapa sabase badi party ke rup main ubharegi lekin yah anumaan sapa netaaon ko bhi nahin tha ki vah 220 ke aankade ko paar karegi
 This performance of the SP, which won a total of 97 seats in the year 2007, surprised the political pundits
 vahiin basapa, jisane pichley chunaav main shandaar 206 siten jitkar pehali baar apane dam par sarkaar banaai thi, uskaa pradarshan behad niraashajanak rahaa
 Thanking the people for the massive victory of SP, Akhilesh Yadav said that the public has expressed confidence in SP by rising above caste and religion
 unki party kii sarkaar janata kii ummiido par khara utarane kii puri koshish karegi
 He said, "the SP will implement its full manifesto after forming the government, so that Uttar Pradesh can go on the path of prosperity and development
 " Akhilesh said, "tomorrow (wednesday) there will be a meeting of the party parliamentary party
 baithak ke baad tay hoga ki sarkaar banane kaa daawa kab pesh kiya jaae
 " samarthan ke bare main puche jane par akhilesh ne saaf kaha, "ham kisi mafia kaa samarthan nahin lenge
 "he said," On the issue of law and order, we had to clean the public during the entire election, but we assure the public that strict action will be taken against the person who breaks the law in the SP government
 " Akhilesh said, "neither an idol of an elephant will be pierced nor will an idol of Chief Minister Mayawati be broken
 hamaari sarkaar badale kii bhaavana ke tahat karwai nahin karegi
 "he also said," If educational institutions or hospitals are opened in the empty space of parks and monuments, then people will benefit
 " On the question of who will become the chief minister, Akhilesh said, "the whole party wants the leader (mulayam) to become the chief minister, so he will become the same
" " Though disappointed with the performance in the elections, it may be a relief for the BJP to come in third place, but the result is a big setback for the Congress, which has fielded its 'yuvraj' Rahul Gandhi with full preparation in the state politics
 congress raibareli jile kii sabhi siton par parajeet ho chuki he
